SELECT [v].[VehicleId], [v].[CompanyId], [v].[CreateBy], [v].[CreateDate], [v].[DateAdded], [v].[DeleteBy], [v].[DeleteDate], [v].[DeleteFlag], [v].[Description], [v].[Image], [v].[ModelNumber], [v].[Name], [v].[Status], [v].[SupplierId], [v].[UpdateBy], [v].[UpdateDate], [s].[SupplierId], [s].[Address], [s].[BankAccount], [s].[BankName], [s].[ContactPerson], [s].[ContractDate], [s].[ContractNumber], [s].[CreateBy], [s].[CreateDate], [s].[DeleteBy], [s].[DeleteDate], [s].[DeleteFlag], [s].[Email], [s].[Notes], [s].[PhoneNumber], [s].[Status], [s].[SupplierName], [s].[TaxCode], [s].[UpdateBy], [s].[UpdateDate], [s].[Website], [c].[CompanyId], [c].[CompanyName], [c].[CreateBy], [c].[CreateDate], [c].[DeleteBy], [c].[DeleteDate], [c].[DeleteFlag], [c].[Email], [c].[PhoneNumber], [c].[Status], [c].[UpdateBy], [c].[UpdateDate]
